古今图书集成医部全录卷四百三十四

小儿吐泻门

　　　　小儿直诀 【宋　钱乙】

　　　　　吐泻兼变证治

　　五月二十五日以后，吐泻壮热，此脏腑中九分热也。伤热乳食，吐而不消，泻色深黄，玉露散主之。　　六月十五日以后，吐泻身温，脏腑六分冷也。呕吐乳食不消，泻色黄白，口干作渴者，食前少服益黄散，食后多服玉露散。　　七月七日以后，吐泻身凉，三分热七分冷也。不乳多睡，闷乱哽气，出气，睡卧露睛，唇白多哕，亦用益黄、玉露二散主之。　　八月十五日以后，吐泻身凉，不乳干哕，泻青褐水，无阳也，当用益黄散。吐泻乳食不化，时时下痢，肌肉消瘦，此脾胃虚寒也，用木香丸。夏月不可服，如有冷证则少服之。其身温壮热，或泻痢红黄赤黑，此脾胃实热也，用黄连丸。冬月不可服，如有热证，则少服之。[1p]

Collection of Medical Texts from Ancient and Modern Times, Volume 434: Pediatric Vomiting and Diarrhea

Directives for Pediatric Patients (Song Dynasty, Qian Yi)

Treatment for Concurrent Vomiting and Diarrhea

After May 25, vomiting and diarrhea with strong heat indicates nine parts heat in the internal organs. If heat injures milk and food, resulting in vomiting that does not relieve, and diarrhea that is deep yellow in color, Yulu San should be used.

After June 15, vomiting and diarrhea with warm body indicates six parts cold in the internal organs. If there is vomiting of undigested milk and food, diarrhea that is yellow-white, and dryness and thirst, take a small dose of Yihuang San before meals and a larger dose of Yulu San after meals.

After July 7, vomiting and diarrhea with cool body indicates three parts heat and seven parts cold. If not breastfeeding due to excessive sleeping, experiencing agitation and choking, with breathlessness, sleeping with eyes open, and pale lips with frequent belching, both Yihuang and Yulu San should be used.

After August 15, vomiting and diarrhea with cool body, not breastfeeding, dry belching, and diarrhea of dark greenish-brown water indicates lack of yang, and Yihuang San should be used. For persistent diarrhea with undigested milk and food, resulting in muscle atrophy, this indicates spleen and stomach deficiency and coldness, and should use Muxiang Wan. It should not be taken in summer; if there are cold symptoms, take it in small doses.

If the body is warm with strong heat, or diarrhea is red, yellow, or black, this indicates excess heat in the spleen and stomach, and Huanglian Wan should be used. It should not be taken in winter; if there are heat symptoms, take it in small doses.[1p]

　　 【注　按前法即《内经》用寒远寒，用热远热之本旨。又云：有假者反之，虽违其时以从其证。盖胃伤则呕吐，脾伤则泄泻，脾胃俱伤则吐泻并作。前证若伤辛热，停滞呕吐，或大便下痢者，用六君子加黄连、吴茱萸、木香。若停滞已去，泄泻不已，用四君子加肉蔻、骨脂。若伤生冷腹痛，泻痢青白，用六君子加砂仁、木香、炮姜。若伤鱼肉等物，用六君子加山楂、砂仁。若泻红黄赤黑，诸脏皆热也，先用香连丸，后用补中益气汤送香连丸。若泻痢青白、乳食不化者，用人参理中丸。若吐泻昏睡而露睛者，用五味异功散。睡而不露睛者，用玉露散。若吐而手足俱热，或喜冷饮食，或睡不露睛者，用泻黄散。或手足冷，或恶冷饮食，或睡而露睛者，用六君子、木香。[2p]

Note: According to previous methods as per the "Inner Canon," if there is cold, use distant cold; if heat, use distant heat. It is also said that if there is stagnation, treat it in opposition, even if it contradicts the timing but aligns with the symptoms. The stomach injury will cause vomiting, the spleen injury will lead to diarrhea, and if both the spleen and stomach are injured, vomiting and diarrhea will occur together. For symptoms of damage from pungent heat, with stagnation causing vomiting or severe diarrhea, use Six Gentlemen Decoction plus Huanglian, Wuzhuyu, and Muxiang. If the stagnation has resolved but diarrhea persists, use Four Gentlemen Decoction plus Muxiang and Guozhi. If caused by injury from consuming cold, resulting in abdominal pain and greenish-white diarrhea, use Six Gentlemen Decoction plus Sharen, Muxiang, and Paojiang. If the injury is due to fish or meat, use Six Gentlemen Decoction plus Hawthorn and Sharen. If the diarrhea is red, yellow, or of any dark color, indicating general heat in the organs, first use Xianglian Pill, then follow with Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction to aid the Xianglian Pill. If experiencing greenish-white diarrhea, or if milk and food are undigested, use Ren Shen Li Zhong Pill. If there is vomiting and significant drowsiness with open eyes, use Wuwei Yigong Powder. If drowsiness without open eyes, use Yulu Powder. If there is vomiting with both hands and feet being hot, or if there is a preference for cold food and drink, or if drowsiness without open eyes, use Xie Huang Powder. If hands and feet are cold, if there is aversion to cold food and drink, or if there is drowsiness with open eyes, use Six Gentlemen Decoction and Muxiang.[2p]

然木香、黄连二丸，虽能攻病克邪，不无伤损脾胃，治者审之！】　　若吐乳泻黄，伤热乳也；吐乳泻青，伤冷乳也，皆当下之。吐泻昏倦，睡不露晴者，胃实热也。吐痰涎及绿水者，胃虚冷也。　　 【注　按前证若儿自受惊，或乳母恚怒，致儿吐泻青色者，宜用异功散加柴胡。若母食厚味而乳热者，用东垣清胃散。母饮酒而乳热者，用葛花解酲汤，子服一二匙。若饮烧酒而乳热，或子母身赤，或昏愦，服冷米醋三五杯，多亦无妨；儿服一二匙。若母停滞生冷而乳冷者，母服养胃汤，子服调中丸。若母停滞而变热乳者，母服大安丸，子服五味异功散。若母郁怒伤肝脾而乳热者，用归脾汤、逍遥散。若母脾虚血弱而乳热者，用六君子加芎、归。[3p]

The two pills, Mu Xiang and Huang Lian, while capable of dispelling disease and counteracting evil, are not without damage to the spleen and stomach; practitioners should examine accordingly! If one experiences vomiting with a yellow or watery diarrhea, it indicates damage from heat in the milk; if vomiting with a blue or green diarrhea, it indicates damage from cold in the milk; both should be treated with purgatives. Vomiting or diarrhea accompanied by lethargy and an inability to be refreshed by sleep indicates excess heat in the stomach. If there's sputum and green water, it suggests a cold weakness in the stomach.

Note: In cases where a child is startled or when a nursing mother is angry, leading to blue vomiting or diarrhea, it is advisable to use Yi Gong San with Chai Hu. If the mother consumes rich foods causing heat in the milk, use Dong Yuan Qing Wei San. If the mother has drunk alcohol causing heat in the milk, administer Ge Hua Jie Cheng Tang, one or two spoonfuls for the child. If consuming strong liquor causes heat in the milk, or if the mother and child develop redness or cloudiness, taking three to five cups of cold rice vinegar is also beneficial; the child may take one or two spoonfuls. If the mother has stagnation causing cold milk, she should take Yang Wei Tang, while the child should take Tiao Zhong Wan. If the mother has stagnation that heats the milk, she should take Da An Wan, and the child should take Wu Wei Yi Gong San. If the mother is emotionally upset, harming her liver and spleen, leading to hot milk, use Gui Pi Tang or Xiao Yao San. If the mother has a weak spleen and low blood causing heat in the milk, use Liu Jun Zi Tang, adding Chuan Xiong and Gui.[3p]

若母气血虚而乳热者，子母俱服八珍散。若母劳役发热而乳热者，子母俱服补中益气汤。若因母怒动肝火而乳热者，用五味异功散加柴胡、山栀。其吐痰涎及白绿水者，肝木乘脾土之虚寒证也，用六君子加柴胡、木香。大凡吐乳泻青色者属惊，法当平肝补脾；吐泻青白色者属寒，法当温补脾土。前诸证若手足指热者属实，手足指冷者属虚，此亦验法也。】　　初生十日内，吐泻壮热，不乳或乳不消，或白色，先用白饼子下之，后用益黄散和之。　　初生下吐，因秽恶下咽故也，用水瓜散主之。凡初生须急拭净口中，否则啼声一发，秽物咽下，致生诸病。　　 【注　按芽儿初生之患，多因乳母不慎七情，不节厚味，传儿为病，当审其因以调治其母。前所用之药，恐脏腑脆嫩，不能胜受，治者审之！】[4p]

If the mother has deficiency of qi and blood along with heat in the milk, both the mother and child should take the Eight Treasures Powder. If the mother has fever due to overwork and there is heat in the milk, both should take the Middle-Boosting Qi Decoction. If the heat in the milk is due to the mother's anger affecting the liver, use the Five-Flavored Different Effects Powder with added Chai Hu and Shan Zhi. If there is vomiting of phlegm or white-green fluid, it indicates a condition where the liver wood overcomes the spleen earth due to deficiency and cold; use the Six Gentlemen Decoction with added Chai Hu and Mu Xiang. Generally, if there is vomiting of milk and diarrhea with a bluish color, it pertains to fright, and treatment should focus on calming the liver and tonifying the spleen; if the vomiting and diarrhea are bluish-white, it relates to cold, and treatment should involve warm tonification of the spleen earth. If the previous conditions are accompanied by hot hands and feet, it indicates excess; if cold hands and feet, it indicates deficiency, which is also a method of diagnosis.

Within the first ten days after birth, if there is vomiting, diarrhea, and strong heat, and either no milk or milk that cannot be digested, or if it is white, first use the White Biscuit Powder to purge, then follow with the Yi Huang Powder to harmonize.

For newborns experiencing vomiting due to foulness swallowed, use the Water Melon Powder to address it. In general, for newborns, it is essential to promptly clean the mouth; otherwise, as soon as they cry, they may accidentally swallow waste, leading to various illnesses.

(Note: According to the notes, many issues in newborns arise from the wet nurse's lack of caution with emotions and indulgence in rich flavors, transferring illness to the child. One should carefully assess the cause to treat the mother. The medications previously mentioned may be too harsh for the delicate organs and must be used judiciously.)[4p]

　　　　河间六书 【金　刘完素】

　　　　　泻痢

　　五脏皆言热证，无寒冷证，亦有谓泻痢小便青白不濇为寒。水谷不化而色不变，吐痢腥秽，澄澈清冷，青白不濇，身凉不渴，脉迟细而微者寒证也。　　谷虽不化，而色变非白，烦渴，小便黄赤而濇者为热证。世传小儿吐痢霍乱，食乳未及消化而痢尚白，便论为寒证误矣。仲景云：热邪不化谷。岂为寒也！
　　　　儒门事亲 【元　张从政】

　　　　　身热吐泻

　　凡小儿身热吐泻，腹满不进饮食，可急与牛黄通膈丸，下过四五行则自愈矣。盖乳食便属水，甚则成湿，以治湿法治之，用燥热之药非也。　　凡小儿水泄不止，可用五苓散与益元散各停，用新水调下三二钱，频服，不拘时候。若暴速注下，甚者属火，凉膈、通圣等散治之，用者勿轻。非深于造化者，未易语此。[5p]

Hejian Six Classics (by Liu Wanshu)

Diarrhea

All five organs indicate heat syndromes, without signs of cold. However, some say that diarrhea with clear, pale, and non-turbid urine indicates cold. When food and drink do not digest but the color remains unchanged, resulting in foul-smelling vomit and diarrhea that is clear and cool, with pale and non-turbid appearance, and the body feeling cool without thirst, a weak and fine pulse indicates a cold syndrome. Although food does not digest, if the color changes and there is restlessness, thirst, and yellowish-red, turbid urine, it indicates a heat syndrome. It is commonly believed that children suffering from vomiting and diarrhea from cholera, with undigested milk resulting in white diarrhea, is mistakenly considered a cold syndrome. Zhang Zhongjing said: "Heat evil does not digest food." How could it be cold!

Filial Piety in the Confucian School (by Zhang Congzheng)

Body Heat, Vomiting, and Diarrhea

In the case of children with body heat, vomiting, and diarrhea, with abdominal fullness and inability to take in food and drink, one can urgently administer Niu Huang Tong Ge Wan. If the condition persists beyond four or five doses, recovery should ensue. This is because dairy foods belong to the category of water, and if severe, it results in dampness. Treating damp with drying and heating medicines is inappropriate. In cases of persistent watery diarrhea in children, one may use Wuling San and Yiyuan San each, with a dose of three to two qian mixed in fresh water, administered frequently without regard to time. If symptoms worsen rapidly, it pertains to fire, treat with cooling methods such as Qingge and Tongsheng, and those who use them should not take them lightly. This is not easy to explain without deep understanding of nature.[5p]

　　　　　水泻

　　小儿暴注水泻不止，《内经》曰：此名暴速注泻，久而不愈者，为涌泄注下，此乃火运太过之病也。火性暴速故也。急宜用新汲水调下甘露饮子、五苓散、天水散，或用井花水煎此药，放冷服之，病即瘥矣。不可用御米壳、干姜、豆豉圣散子之类，纵然泻止，肠胃气滞不通，变为腹胀。此法宜分阴阳利水道，乃为治法之妙也。
　　　　　久泻不止

　　凡小儿久泻不止，至八九月间，变为秋深冷痢，泄泻青白，时时撮痛，乳瓣不化，可用养脾丸如黍米大，每服二三十丸，米饮送下，日进三服则愈。益黄散亦可用之。　　凡治小儿之法，不可用极寒极热之药，及峻补峻泻之剂，或误用巴豆、杏仁、硫黄、腻粉之药。若用此药，反生他病。小儿易虚易实，肠胃嫩弱，不胜其毒，若治之，宜用分阴阳、利水道最为急，用桂苓甘露散之类。[6p]

Diarrhea

When a child experiences sudden and persistent diarrhea, the "Inner Canon" states that this is called acute diarrhea. If it persists and does not improve, it is due to excessive fire in the body. The nature of fire is abrupt and rapid. It is urgent to use freshly drawn water to prepare drinks such as Ganlu (sweet dew) and Wuling powder, or Tian Shui powder. Alternatively, one can decoct these medicines in well water, let it cool, and have the patient take it, which will lead to recovery. One should avoid cold rice husk, dried ginger, and strong purgative herbs; even if the diarrhea is stopped, it may cause stagnation in the intestines and stomach, leading to abdominal distension. The treatment must differentiate between yin and yang and promote the water pathways, which is the essence of effective treatment.

Persistent Diarrhea

If a child suffers from prolonged diarrhea that persists until eight or nine months, it may develop into cold dysentery in autumn, characterized by cyanotic and white diarrhea, frequent pain, and undigested milk. One can use Yangpi pills about the size of millet, taking two to thirty pills each time, washed down with rice drink, three times a day until recovery. Yihuang powder may also be used.

In general, when treating children, one must avoid extreme cold or extreme hot medications, as well as harsh tonics and purgatives, or mistakenly using physic such as croton seeds, apricot kernels, sulfur, or greasy powders. Using these may cause additional illnesses. As children are prone to weakness and strong reactions, their intestines and stomach are tender and cannot withstand toxicity. When treating them, it is imperative to use methods that differentiate between yin and yang and promote water pathways, with preparations like Guiling Ganlu powder being particularly urgent.[6p]

　　　　幼科全书 【元　朱震亨】

　　　　　呕吐

　　有物无声曰吐，有声无物曰呕，有声有物曰呕吐。其证有三，有寒、有热、有食积伤。　　凡寒吐者，吐时少而出物多，此胃家受寒也。或用胃苓丸，煨姜汤吞，或以理中丸治之。寒吐食不化，不恶食。　　凡热吐者，吐时多而出物少，此胃家有热也。以二陈汤加黄连、煨干姜治之。热吐食化，不恶食。　　凡食积吐者，要分三焦明白，俱能食。如食时即吐者，此积在上焦胃口也，宜用淡盐汤吞下，后用鹅翎毛扫口中，令其吐尽旧积，以二陈汤加煨干姜、神曲、炒麦芽、炒杏仁治之。　　如食下一二时而吐者，此积在中焦胃下口过小肠上口处也。先以丁香脾积丸通去旧积，后以二陈汤加消导药治之。[7p]

Treatment of Vomiting

There are three types of vomiting: silent vomiting, which is devoid of material; noisy vomiting, which has no material; and vomiting with both sound and material. The conditions are categorized into three: cold, heat, and food accumulation.

For cold vomiting, the expulsion is small while the quantity is large; this indicates that the stomach is affected by cold. One may use Wei Ling Wan or ginger decoction to swallow, or treat with Li Zhong Wan. In cases of cold vomiting, food does not congeal, and there is no aversion to food.

For heat vomiting, one expels a large quantity with little material; this indicates that the stomach is hot. Treat with Er Chen Tang combined with Huang Lian and cooked ginger. In heat vomiting, food is digested, and there is no aversion to food.

For food accumulation vomiting, it is essential to identify the three burners clearly, as all can consume food. If one vomits immediately upon eating, the accumulation is in the upper burner (stomach), and one should swallow with light salt water and afterward use a goose feather to clean the mouth to expel any residual accumulation, treating with Er Chen Tang combined with cooked ginger, Shen Qu, stir-fried malt, and stir-fried almonds.

If vomiting occurs one to two hours after eating, the accumulation is in the middle burner (gastric outlet near the small intestine). First use Ding Xiang Pi Ji Wan to clear the old accumulation, then treat with Er Chen Tang combined with digestive medicines.[7p]

　　如早食晚吐，晚食早吐者，此食在下焦，小肠口下过大肠口上处也。先以丁香脾积丸下之，后以二陈汤加消导药治之。消草药如神曲、麦芽、砂仁、香附之类。如呕吐久而诸药不纳者，此胃口伏火关格之病，用理中汤加童便、猪胆汁同炒煎服即止，神效，妙不可言。　　如呕吐出蛔虫者，以理中汤加乌梅一个，附子一小片，黄蘗、川椒一服即止。　　如呕吐后而瘦弱者，只以集圣丸调之。　　如诸吐不纳药者，此阴盛拒阳也；必加童便、猪胆者，盖童便味酸咸性寒，胆汁味苦性寒，以和理中汤服，则阴体渐消，阳性乃发，此《内经》所云：伏其所主先其所因也，非吾子孙不示。　　凡吐不止，目上视，头后仰者不治。　　袓传治呕吐，只用胃苓丸，煨姜汤送下，不问寒热皆效。凡吐不止，服药无效，更加烦闷，不治。　　西江月[8p]

If one experiences early morning vomiting after breakfast or vomiting after an evening meal, it indicates that the food is stuck in the lower jiao, below the small intestine and above the large intestine. First, administer the Dingxiang Pine Accumulation Pill to alleviate this issue, then use the Erchen Decoction combined with digestive herbs to treat it. Digestive herbs such as Shenyu, Malt, Sand Ginger, and Xiangfu should be included. If vomiting persists and none of the medicines are being absorbed, this indicates a condition of concealed stomach fire obstructing the entrance; in this case, use the Lizhong Decoction combined with children's urine and pig bile, stir-fry and prepare it for consumption, which will stop the issue effectively—its efficacy is remarkable and inexpressible.

If one vomits up roundworms, use the Lizhong Decoction with one black plum, a little piece of Aconite, and Huangbo and Chuan Jiao to stop it. If one becomes weak after vomiting, simply adjust with the Jisheng Pill. If various vomits are unable to absorb medicine, it indicates a deficiency of Yang due to excess Yin; adding children’s urine and pig bile is essential, as children’s urine is sour and salty with a cold nature, while bile is bitter and cold, which harmonizes with the Lizhong Decoction. This way, Yin gradually disperses and Yang can emerge; this aligns with what the Inner Canon states about addressing the root cause before the symptoms—this knowledge is not for my descendants to reveal.

In cases of persistent vomiting with eyes looking upwards and head leaning back, do not treat. The ancestral method for treating vomiting simply employs the Weiling Pill, taken with ginger decoction, effective regardless of hot or cold. If vomiting continues, taking medication yields no effect, and the patient becomes increasingly agitated, do not treat further.[8p]

　　呕吐饮食不纳，任从汤药难尝。此为阴盛隔孤阳，到是时医魔障。参朮煨姜熟附，乌梅童便尤良。猪胆同入慢精详，此法应如影向。　　一等蛔虫吐出，此为蛔厥多阴。乌梅丸子效如神，一服蛔安吐定。又有咳而呕者，化痰顺气须明。如常吐呕只胃苓，汤用煨姜作引。[9p]

Vomiting and refusal of food make it hard for medicine to take effect. This is due to excessive yin blocking the solitary yang, making it the time for medical troubles. Ginseng and astragalus cooked with ginger and served hot, and black plum with child’s urine are especially good. Adding pig bile in a careful manner, this method should respond like a shadow.

First, expel the roundworm; this is due to roundworm causing excessive yin. The black plum pill works like a miracle; a single dose will stabilize the stomach and stop vomiting. For those who cough and then vomit, transforming phlegm and smoothing qi is essential. If regularly experiencing vomiting, use ginger in the soup as a guide.[9p]

　　　　　泄泻

　　凡泄泻皆属湿，其证有五，治法以分利升提为主，不可一例混施。如泄泻青白，或乳食不化，肠痛四肢冷，面晃白不作渴者，此寒湿也。其证多得于冬，以五苓散作引，吞化理中丸即止。如寒甚不止者，理中汤加附子一片即效。　　如泄泻黄稠，腹痛作热，面红口渴，此热湿也，其证多得于夏，以五苓散加滑石、甘草、木通治之，甚者以玉露散、理中汤即效。　　如泄泻不住成黄水者，或渴或不渴，此风湿也，其证多得于夏，以五苓散加防风、苍朮、羌活治之。　　如久泻肠滑不止者，此湿伤元气下陷也，宜升提之药，四君子汤加升麻、防风、乌梅治之，或用四君子汤吞下七味肉豆蔻丸亦效。[10p]

Diarrhea

Diarrhea is generally related to dampness, with five types of symptoms. The main treatment method focuses on promoting elimination and lifting, and one should not apply the same treatment indiscriminately. For symptoms of diarrhea with a pale blue color, or undigested dairy and food, accompanied by abdominal pain and cold limbs, with a pale face and no thirst, this is cold dampness. Symptoms often arise in winter, and one should use Wuling Powder as a guide, swallowing the Lizhong Pill to stop the condition. If the cold is severe and does not stop, Li Zhong Decoction with a slice of Fuzi will be effective.

For diarrhea characterized by yellow and thick stools, abdominal pain with heat, a red face, and thirst, this is heat dampness. Symptoms usually occur in summer, and one should treat it with Wuling Powder supplemented with Talcum, Licorice, and Mutong; in severe cases, Yulu San or Li Zhong Decoction will be effective.

For persistent diarrhea resulting in yellow watery stools, with or without thirst, this is wind dampness. Symptoms commonly occur in summer, and one should treat it with Wuling Powder combined with Fangfeng, Cangzhu, and Qianghuo.

For chronic diarrhea with slippery intestines that does not stop, this indicates dampness harming the original qi leading to sinking. It is advisable to use herbs that promote lifting. Four Gentlemen Decoction with added Shengma, Fangfeng, and Wumei is recommended, or one can use Four Gentlemen Decoction and swallow Qiwemeiren Doukou Pill to achieve the desired effect.[10p]

　　如泄泻酸臭，腹痛，面黄带热，不喜饮食者，此食积也，先以丁香脾积丸推去其积，后以集圣丸调之。　　如泄泻久，作渴不止者，只以白朮散多煎服之。未有不效者。　　如泄泻久，目无神，口略张，四肢冷，好睡，以四君子汤调之，多服有效；甚者加熟附子一小片，煨干姜服之。　　如泄泻久，身热不退者，只以调元汤治之，此虚热也，不可妄用寒凉之药，甚者加煨干姜即效。　　凡泄泻后，人事黄弱者，只用集圣散服之。　　袓传治泄泻不问寒热，只用胃苓丸兼一粒金丹，以车前子同炒米汤治之。　　凡治久泄不止，精神美好，面赤唇红者，不治；变成白痢者，不治；脉沉细，遍身皮冷，不乳食，作渴不止者，不治；又成惊搐者不治；大孔如竹筒不收闭者，不治；滑泄不止者，不治；大肉消瘦者，不治。　　凡治泄泻，不问轻重，只要乳食如常，不生他证者则易愈。　　清江引[11p]

If there is diarrhea accompanied by a sour smell, abdominal pain, a yellow complexion with heat, and a lack of appetite, this indicates food accumulation. First, use Clove Spleen Accumulation Pill to dispel the accumulation, and then adjust with Gather the Saints Pill.

If diarrhea lasts long and there is unquenchable thirst, just take a decoction of Atractylodes more frequently, and there will be no failure.

If diarrhea persists, the eyes lack spirit, the mouth is slightly open, the limbs feel cold, and there is a desire to sleep, use Four Gentlemen Decoction for adjustment in a larger quantity for effectiveness; for severe cases, add a small piece of cooked Aconite and take with dried ginger.

If diarrhea lasts long with persistent body heat, treat it with Tonic Decoction; as this is due to empty heat, cold or cooling medicines must not be carelessly used, and for severe cases, adding dried ginger will be effective.

For those who appear weak and yellow after diarrhea, just use Gather the Saints Powder.

Traditionally, diarrhea was treated without concern for cold or heat, merely using Stomach Tonic Pills along with one grain of Golden Pill, treating it with a decoction of prepared millet with plantain seeds.

For prolonged diarrhea with good spirit, a red face, and red lips, do not treat; if it turns into dysentery, do not treat; if the pulse is deep and thin, the body feels cold, there is lack of appetite, and thirst is unending, do not treat; if there are convulsions, do not treat; if the stools are as large as bamboo tubes and do not close, do not treat; if there is continuous slippery diarrhea, do not treat; if there is significant weight loss, do not treat.

In general, when treating diarrhea, regardless of severity, as long as dairy and food are consumed as usual and no other symptoms arise, recovery is easy.

　　夏月人多泄泻，腹痛烦渴相攻。猪苓泽泻茯苓同，甘草干姜多用。白朮黄连滑石，人参砂藿温中。升麻提气妙无穷，更把乌梅煎送。　　夏月雨多伤湿，宜利小便为先。猪苓泽泻与黄连，栀子茵陈解散。羌活青皮枳实，茯苓赤者相参。木瓜苍白朮同煎，黄蘗加些灵验。　　泄泻秘传治法，等闲不语时人。如今传授与儿孙，胜似良田万顷。初次且行淡渗，温中以次施行。三升四塞救孩婴，此法古今永定。　　泄泻缘何发作，只因水谷无分。所以淡渗法先行，小便长而泄定。滑石车前赤茯，人参白朮猪苓。甘草泽泻与砂仁，姜枣煎时作引。　　淡渗行而还泄，须防谷气中虚。温中丸散不须拘，但要一时泄住。白朮人参砂藿，炙姜炙草依书。乌梅熟附泽苓猪，引用枣姜作主。　　温中若犹不效，中气下陷须提。人参白朮与黄芪，甘草干姜炙取。[13p]

　　　　　吐泻

　　吐泻之证有三，有寒有热有积，治法略与泄门相似，观者详之。　　凡吐泻两腮红，足胫热，好饮水，身上热，此热证也。治法以胃苓丸、一粒金丹，同车前草灯心汤送下。　　凡吐泻面晃白，足胫冷，不作渴，如有热者，此寒证也。治法先以理中汤即止，不止便以益黄散治之，或胃苓丸、肉豆蔻丸治之。　　凡吐泻恶食或不乳，心腹痛，吐泻所出之物皆酸臭，此食积也。先去食积，以感应丸推之，后以胃苓丸调之，或食脾积丸亦可。　　凡吐泻日久渐渐瘦弱，作渴作热，久不治，必成坏证，用加减补中汤治之。　　西江月[15p]

Vomiting and Diarrhea

There are three types of symptoms for vomiting and diarrhea: cold, heat, and accumulation. The treatment methods are somewhat similar to those for diarrhea; those observing should examine them closely.

In cases of vomiting and diarrhea with flushed cheeks, warm legs and feet, a preference for drinking water, and a hot body, this indicates a heat condition. The treatment method is to use Weiling Pills or a single Jin Dan, administered with Cheqian Grass and Dengxin Decoction.

In cases of vomiting and diarrhea with a pale face, cold legs and feet, and lack of thirst, and if there is any heat present, this indicates a cold condition. The treatment is to start with Lizhong Decoction to stop the symptoms, and if they don’t stop, then use Yihuang Powder, or treat with Weiling Pills or Rou Dou Kou Pills.

In cases of vomiting and diarrhea where there is aversion to food or inability to breastfeed, accompanied by abdominal pain, and the vomit and diarrhea are all sour and foul, this indicates food accumulation. First, remove the food accumulation using the Ganying Pills, then regulate with Weiling Pills, or alternatively, Food Spleen Accumulation Pills may also be effective.

In cases of prolonged vomiting and diarrhea where one gradually becomes thinner and weaker, experiences thirst and heat, and if not treated for a long time, it will certainly worsen. For this, use a modified Buzhong Decoction for treatment.[15p]

　　大凡男女吐泻。阴阳顺逆当明。男逢泄盛下无阴，女子吐多不应。出物多而数少，此为寒食相侵。如逢物少数频频，火盛细加体认。　　吐泻若然同见，此名霍乱阴阳，只消一贴理中汤，上吐下泻了当。服药若还不效，再加熟附煨姜。乌梅作引是良方，莫与俗人夸奖。　　吐泻时时作渴，诸般汤药无灵。饮汤饮水腹肿膨，束手待观死定。急饮茯苓饮子，时时与儿调停。须臾吐止火邪宁，才与理中对证。
　　　　婴童百问 【明　鲁伯嗣】

　　　　　呕证吐乳证

　　仲阳云：初生下拭掠小儿口中秽恶不尽，咽入喉中，故呕吐及多生诸病。呕者，有声也；吐者，吐出乳也。凡小儿乳哺不宜过饱，若满则溢，故令呕吐。胃中纳乳，如器之盛物，杯桊之小，不可容巨碗之物。雨骤则沼溢，酒暴则卮翻，理之必然。乳母无知，但欲速得乳儿长大，更无时度，或儿睡着而更口　衔乳，岂有厌足？受病之源，自此渐至日深。[16p]

Generally, when men and women suffer from vomiting and diarrhea, the balance of yin and yang should be clear. If a man experiences severe diarrhea without the presence of yin, and a woman vomits excessively without reason, this indicates a conflict caused by cold food. If there is an abundance of material but a scarcity of frequency, this suggests a prevalence of heat that must be carefully recognized.

If vomiting and diarrhea appear simultaneously, this is termed chaotic yang and yin. A single application of the rational remedy will resolve both vomiting and diarrhea. If taking medicine still proves ineffective, add gently processed ginger. Using black plum as an assistant is excellent advice, but do not boast about it to ordinary people.

If vomiting and diarrhea cause persistent thirst, various soups and medicines yield no effect. If drinking soup or water leads to abdominal swelling, one may be resigned to fate, awaiting death. Quickly drink Poria remedy and often mediate for the child. When vomiting ceases, and the fire is soothed, then confirm with the rational remedy.

In the "Hundred Questions of Infants" by Lu Bosi from the Ming Dynasty:

Zhong Yang states: When a newborn is cleaned, if the mouth is not thoroughly cleared of filth, it is swallowed into the throat, resulting in vomiting and various illnesses. "Vomiting" involves a sound, while "to throw up" refers to expelling milk. In general, infants should not be overfed; if full, they will overflow, leading to vomiting. The stomach takes in milk like a vessel filled with things; a small cup cannot hold the volume of a large bowl. When rain falls heavily, a pond overflows; when wine is violently stirred, a cup flips over. This is a matter of logic.

Wet nurses, lacking knowledge, merely focus on quickly getting the child to grow without considering timing; they may continue to feed the child while it sleeps. How can there be satisfaction? The source of illness gradually develops from this.[16p]

导其胃气之虚，慢惊自此而得，可不慎乎？此候但令节乳为上，甚者宜令断乳，先此乳母可服调气之剂，儿服消食丸，化乳壮胃为上。议曰吐乳哯乳，此证有数般，有冷有热，当自辨认。若吐自口角出，此是乳多，消化不及，满而则溢，此非病也，常服消乳丸、异功散，当令乳母节乳为上。冷吐可服亲音散、香朴散、快脾等药，热吐则头额温，有黄涎而渴，小便赤少，此是热吐，多是伤暑热者有此证，乳母同服香薷散、五苓散。又有风痰吐，乃是伤风不解，吐乳夹痰，若经久必然生风，仍宜下疏风化痰药，竹茹汤去桂、五苓散、青州白丸子、温胆汤。又当留心调治，紫霜丸亦可服。
　　　　　热吐

　　小儿秋夏伏暑，多有热吐。何以别之？或有黄涎，头额温，五心热，小便赤而少，或唇干而烦渴，先令乳母服香薷散、五苓散，儿服竹茹汤、五苓散。热甚者大柴胡汤去大黄服，或小柴胡汤亦可。热极者，可服大承气汤，其效如神；玉露散亦可服。[17p]

If the stomach qi is deficient, and this leads to a slow reaction, should one not be cautious? In this case, it’s best to control the milk supply, and if it’s severe, to cease breastfeeding altogether. Initially, the wet nurse can take tonics to regulate the qi, while the child should take digestion pills to transform milk and strengthen the stomach. It is stated that issues such as vomiting milk may arise under various conditions, with both cold and heat manifestations, and one must discern the differences. If the milk comes out from the corners of the mouth, it indicates an excess of milk that the child cannot digest, leading to overflow; this is not a disease. Regular use of milk-dissolving pills or various tonics is advisable, and it is crucial for the wet nurse to moderate her milk supply. For cold-induced vomiting, remedies such as Qinyin Decoction, Xiangfu Powder, and Kuai Pi should be administered. If the vomiting is due to heat, the forehead will feel warm, with yellow saliva and thirst, and the urine will be scant and red. This is indicative of heat-induced vomiting, often seen after overheating. The wet nurse should also take Xiangru Powder and Wuling Powder. Additionally, for phlegm-induced vomiting due to unresolved wind, if the child vomits milk with phlegm, and this persists over time, it may lead to wind conditions; thus, one should consider laxative and phlegm-dissolving medicines, such as Zhu Ru Decoction without cinnamon, Wuling Powder, Qingzhou White Pills, and Warm Gallbladder Decoction. Careful adjustment and treatment should be prioritized, and Zishuang Pill may also be taken.

Heat-induced vomiting

During autumn and summer, children often experience heat-induced vomiting. How can one distinguish this? Symptoms may include yellow saliva, a warm forehead, heat in the five palms, scant and red urine, or dry lips accompanied by restlessness and thirst. The wet nurse should first take Xiangru Powder and Wuling Powder, while the child takes Zhu Ru Decoction and Wuling Powder. In cases of severe heat, a modified Chai Hu Decoction without Da Huang can be used, or Xiao Chai Hu Decoction may also be effective. For extreme heat, Da Cheng Qi Decoction may be administered, and its effects are remarkable; Yu Lu Powder can also be taken.[17p]

　　　　　寒冷呕吐哕逆

　　小儿感受风冷，或食生冷瓜果过多，胃口停寒，以致吐食吐乳，并用理中汤主之；或酿乳法、消乳丸、异功散、香朴散、茯苓半夏汤、二陈汤、人参散、麝沉散，俱可服。
　　　　　霍乱吐泻

　　小儿吐泻，有身温者，有身热者，有身凉者，有吐泻成惊风者，有夏月伤暑吐泻者，有初生三日内吐泻者。仲阳云：小儿初生三日内，吐泻壮热，不思乳食，大便青白，乳食不消，或白色，是伤寒，当下之；后和胃，仍用白饼子。和胃用益黄散主之。三日以后至十日，吐泻身温凉，不思乳食，大便青白色，乳食不消，此上实下虚也，用益黄散加减治之。又伤风吐泻身温，乍凉乍热，多气，兼大便黄白色，呕吐乳食不消，时时咳嗽，更有五脏兼见证，当服入脏君臣药，先大青膏后益黄散主之。[18p]

Cold Vomiting and Reversal

If a child is affected by wind and cold, or consumes too much raw or cold fruits, the stomach may become cold, resulting in vomiting food or milk. This can be treated with the Rilizhong Decoction; other remedies include the Milk Fermentation Method, Digestive Tablets, Yigong Powder, Xiangpu Powder, Fuling Banxia Decoction, Erchen Decoction, Ren Shen Powder, and Shechen Powder.

Cholera with Vomiting and Diarrhea

For children who experience vomiting and diarrhea, some may have a warm body, while others may feel hot or cool. There are those whose vomiting and diarrhea cause convulsions, those that suffer from summer heat, and those who vomit or have diarrhea within three days of birth. It is said: If a child under three days old has vomiting and diarrhea with strong heat, lacks desire for milk or food, has blue-white stools, and cannot digest milk or food, it indicates a cold damage, and should be purged immediately; afterward, warm the stomach with white biscuits. To warm the stomach, use Yihuang Powder as the primary treatment.

From three to ten days later, if vomiting and diarrhea occur with a warm or cool body, lacking desire for milk or food, and blue-white stools with undigested milk or food, this indicates excess above and deficiency below; treat it with adjusted Yihuang Powder. Additionally, if there is a wind-damage with vomiting and diarrhea, presenting warm at times and cool at others, with much qi, and yellow-white stools, along with vomiting undigested milk or food, persistent coughing, and signs affecting the five organs, medicinally, one should use the Junchen medicine, starting with Daqing Ointment and then Yihuang Powder as the primary treatment.[18p]

又吐泻身热多睡，能食乳，饮水不止，吐痰，大便黄水，皆为胃虚热渴吐泻也，当生胃中津液以止其渴，止后用发散药。止渴，多服白朮散；发散，大青膏、钓藤饮主之。又吐泻身凉，吐沫，泻青白色，闷乱不渴，哽气长出气，睡露睛，此伤风荏苒轻怯因成吐泻，当补脾，后发散。补脾，益黄散；发散，大青膏、钓藤饮。夏至后，吐泻身壮热，热证也，或因伤热，乳食呕吐不消，泻深黄色，玉露散主之，五苓散亦佳，香薷散、车前子散可选而用之。若面色青黄，知风热在脾，发直怕人，眼不合，是心中有毒涎，更胃逆风搐，可服定命丹。[19p]

If there is vomiting and diarrhea, high body temperature, excessive sleep, the ability to eat milk, persistent thirst, vomiting phlegm, and yellow watery stools, this indicates stomach deficiency with heat, thirst, and vomiting. One should generate fluids in the stomach to quench the thirst, and after that, use diaphoretic medicines. To quench thirst, frequently take Bai Zhu San; to disperse, use Da Qing Gao and Diao Teng Yin.

If there is vomiting and diarrhea, coolness of the body, foaming at the mouth, pale watery stools, discomfort without thirst, and shortness of breath, this is caused by a slight injury from wind leading to vomiting and diarrhea. One should tonify the spleen and then disperse. To tonify the spleen, use Yi Huang San; for dispersal, Da Qing Gao and Diao Teng Yin.

After the summer solstice, if there is vomiting and diarrhea with strong body heat, this indicates heat syndrome, possibly caused by excessive heat from food, leading to undigested milk causing vomiting and deep yellow diarrhea. Yu Lu San is the main remedy, and Wu Ling San is also good, with options like Xiang Ru San and Che Qian Zi San as alternatives.

If the complexion is greenish-yellow, it indicates wind-heat in the spleen, fear of people, and inability to close the eyes, suggesting there is toxic phlegm in the heart leading to stomach inversion. One can take Ding Ming Dan.[19p]

　　　　　冷泻

　　汤氏云：此乃脾虚受冷，致令水谷不化，泄泻注下。仲阳云：小儿不能食乳，泻褐水，身冷无阳也，当治脾，益黄散主之。古今不同，当依加减法用之，始为稳当。冷积泻，没石子丸极效，人参散、理中汤加减，服尤佳；更加肉豆蔻则止。来复丹、不换金正气散皆可。观音散、银白散加减调治，乃平和之剂也。[20p]

Cold Diarrhea

Tang said: This is due to spleen deficiency caused by cold, leading to the inability to digest food, resulting in diarrhea. Zhong Yang said: When a child cannot digest milk, has brown watery stools, and feels cold with no warmth, one should treat the spleen. Yi Huang San is the main prescription for this. There are differences between ancient and modern approaches, so adjustments should be made according to specific conditions for safety. For cold accumulation diarrhea, the Yan Shi Zi Wan is very effective. Ren Shen San and Li Zhong Tang with modifications are particularly beneficial; adding nutmeg will help stop the symptoms. Lai Fu Dan and Bu Huan Jin Zheng Qi San are also suitable. Guan Yin San and Yin Bai San with adjustments can be used as balanced remedies.[20p]

　　　　　热泻

　　汤氏曰：小儿热泻者，大便黄而赤，或有沫，乃脏中有积，或因乳母好饮酒，或嗜热物，或坐下伤温蕴热，医者不明，但用豆蔻、诃子等药服之，如水浇石，既不识其证，故不辨其冷热，用药又不得其法，焉得取效？此证当以小便赤少，口干烦躁为验。治法当用钱氏白朮散去木香用之，五苓散去桂亦可服。其热甚者，四逆散、大柴胡汤去大黄，服之殊验也。更用黄连丸等剂亦佳。调中汤去大黄加黄连、枳壳。如夹热而泻，太阳与少阳合病，自下利者，与黄芩汤，呕者加半夏也。又有挟热泻利而小便秘濇赤甚者，四顺清凉饮主之。[21p]

Heat Diarrhea

Tang's School states: In cases of heat diarrhea in children, the stools are yellow and red, sometimes with foam, indicating accumulation in the intestines. This may be due to the wet nurse enjoying alcohol, indulging in hot foods, or sitting down causing excess heat. If the physician does not understand this, but merely prescribes cardamom, myrobalan, and other medicines, it is like pouring water on stone; lacking in diagnosis, they cannot differentiate between heat and cold, and using the wrong medication results in no effect. This condition should be verified with signs such as scanty red urine and dry mouth with agitation. The treatment principle should involve using Qian's Bai Zhu powder, excluding wood incense. Wu Ling powder, excluding cassia, can also be taken. For severe heat, Si Ni San or Da Chai Hu Decoction, excluding rhubarb, would be particularly effective. Additionally, Huang Lian Wan and similar formulas are also beneficial. The Tuning Middle Decoction, excluding rhubarb and adding Huang Lian and Zhi Ke, can be used. If there is concurrent heat and diarrhea, with a combination of Tai Yang and Shao Yang diseases and bowel movements, Huang Qin Decoction may be appropriate, adding Ban Xia in cases of vomiting. Furthermore, for cases of heat diarrhea with severe red and scanty urine, Si Shun Qing Liang Drink should be the main remedy.[21p]

　　　　　伤食泻

　　汤氏云：凡此泻不宜便补，先用消食药，或用紫霜丸，取其积尽，然后可补。经云：食泻重当取，疳虚用补虚。治食泻，与香橘饼子、加减观音散、调中汤散，以意加减。凡伤食泻不可即止，宜节饮食，当用进食丸取下食积令尽；次以钱氏加减益黄散，只一服可止，此乃切要治法。然后异功散、四君子汤调理，必取全安。有腹中雷鸣下利者，生姜泻心汤主之。如冷积酿泻，用香朴散止之。白朮散以和气调胃，调中散、保安丸能止伤食泻，感应丸、沉香煎、三棱煎皆可服。[22p]

Food-Related Diarrhea

Tang said: For this type of diarrhea, one should not supplement immediately. First, use digestive medicines or Zishuang Pills to eliminate any food accumulation before considering supplementation. The classics say: For food-related diarrhea, it's important to extract what is heavy, while for weakness from malnutrition, one should utilize tonic herbs. When treating food-related diarrhea, you can use Xiangji Cake, Jiajiang Guanyin Powder, and Tiaozhong Decoction, adjusting as needed. It is essential that food-related diarrhea should not be abruptly stopped; moderation in diet is necessary. Progress with food retention pills to eliminate the accumulated food, followed by Qian’s Jiajiang Yihuang Powder, which can be effective in just one dose—this is a crucial treatment method. Following this, use Yigong Powder or Sijunzi Decoction for recovery to ensure full safety. For those with abdominal rumbling and diarrhea, Shengjiang Xiaoxin Decoction is indicated. If it is a case of cold accumulation causing diarrhea, use Xiangpu Powder to stop it. Baizhu Powder can harmonize qi and regulate the stomach; Tiaozhong Powder and Bao’an Pills can stop food-related diarrhea, while Ganying Pills, Chenxiang Decoction, and Sanling Decoction are also applicable.[22p]

　　　　　惊泻

　　仲阳云：慢惊病后，或吐泻胃虚，或气弱因惊，眼白如淡墨，下粪青黄，此泻合温补，至圣保命丹、钓藤饮主之。或乳随粪下，消乳丸、进食丸主之。或微渴，心脾喘躁狂热，此泻尤难治，辰砂五苓散主之。冷者定命饮子主之，后与温惊朱君散、睡惊太乙丹。
　　　　保婴撮要 【明　薛铠】

　　　　　霍乱吐泻

　　钱仲阳云：吐泻壮热不食，或乳不消，是伤乳也，宜白饼子下之后，用益黄散和胃。若吐泻身温不乳，大便青白。此上实下虚也，用益黄散加减治之。大凡吐泻身温，乍凉乍热，气粗大便黄，自吐乳不消，此伤风热也，先服大青膏发散，后服益黄散和胃。若吐泻身热，多睡能乳，吐痰，大便黄水，胃虚也，先用白朮散生津止渴，后用大青膏、钓藤饮发散风邪。若夏至后吐泻身热，或吐乳泻黄，此伤热乳也，用玉露散之类。[23p]

Surprise Diarrhea

Zhongyang says: After a slow onset of surprise illness, one might vomit and have diarrhea due to stomach deficiency, or feel weak due to fright; with white in the eyes resembling light ink and feces being greenish-yellow, this diarrhea should be treated with warming and tonifying remedies, primarily using the Sacred Life Preservation Pill and the Diaoteng Decoction. If there is milk alongside the feces, it can be treated with the Milk Dissolving Pill or the Eating Enhancement Pill. If there is slight thirst, with heart and spleen symptoms leading to agitation and frenzy, this diarrhea is particularly difficult to treat; use the cinnabar Wuling powder. For cold cases, prescribe the Determining Life Decoction, followed by the Warm Surprise Pill from Zhu Jun and the Sleep-Inducing Great Unity Pill.

Cholera Vomiting and Diarrhea

Qian Zhongyang says: Vomiting and diarrhea with strong heat and lack of appetite, or undigested milk indicates injury to the milk, thus one should take Werther's Cake after which use Yihuang Powder to harmonize the stomach. If there’s vomiting and diarrhea with body heat but no milk, and the stools are greenish-white, this indicates excess above and deficiency below; use Yihuang Powder with adjustments to treat it. Generally, vomiting and diarrhea with body heat, alternating between cool and heat sensations, coarse energy, and yellow stools, along with vomiting undigested milk indicates a wind-heat injury; start with Daqing Gao to disperse, then take Yihuang Powder to harmonize the stomach. If there is a fever with vomiting and diarrhea after the summer solstice, or if undigested milk leads to yellow diarrhea, it indicates injury to the heat of the milk; treat it with Yulu powder or similar preparations.[23p]

凡泻乳腹痛按之而哭者，食积痛也，用白饼子下之；按之不哭者，脾胃气虚也，用五味异功散补之。手足指冷者，脾气虚寒也，用异功散加木香。伤风吐泻者，风木克脾土也，亦用前药。若饮热乳而泻黄者，湿热壅滞也，用四苓散。如不愈或反甚者，元气复伤也，用白朮散。泻而腹中重坠者，脾气下陷也，用补中益气汤。若服克滞之剂，而腹中窄狭者，脾气虚痞也，用六君子汤。若面黄泻青，脾虚而肝乘之也，用六君、柴胡、升麻、木香。若多噫泻黄，心脾气虚也，用六君、炮姜、升麻。生下半月旬日内吐者，止宜调治其母，恐婴儿脏腑脆弱，不胜药饵故也。
　　　　古今医统 【明　徐春甫】[24p]

For those with abdominal pain from milk discharge who cry when pressed, it is due to food accumulation; use white cake to alleviate it. If pressing does not cause crying, it is a deficiency of spleen and stomach qi; use Wumei Yigong San to tonify it. For cold hands and feet, it is due to cold spleen qi; use Yigong San with Mu Xiang. If there is a cold wind leading to vomiting and diarrhea, it indicates wind wood harming spleen earth; also use the aforementioned medicine. If one drinks hot milk and has yellow diarrhea, it indicates damp heat stagnation; use Si Ling San. If symptoms do not improve or worsen, it indicates further harm to the original qi; use Baizhu San. If there is diarrhea with a feeling of heaviness in the abdomen, it indicates a sinking of spleen qi; use Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang. If one uses drugs to resolve stagnation but feels constricted in the abdomen, it indicates a deficiency and stagnation of spleen qi; use Liu Jun Zi Tang. If there is a yellow complexion and green diarrhea, it suggests spleen deficiency with liver overacting; use Liu Jun, Chai Hu, Sheng Ma, and Mu Xiang. If there is frequent belching with yellow diarrhea, it indicates a deficiency of heart and spleen qi; use Liu Jun, Pao Jiang, and Sheng Ma. If vomiting occurs within the first fifteen days after birth, it is best to adjust the mother's condition, as the infant's organs are delicate and may not withstand medicinal treatment.[24p]

　　　　　呕吐

　　呕者，有声也；吐者，吐出乳食也。凡小儿乳哺不宜过饱，若满则溢，故令呕吐。乳母无知，但欲速得儿长，更无时度，或儿睡着而强乳，自此受病之源，渐至日深，遂成呕吐。甚者宜渐断乳，先令乳母服调气之剂，儿服消食丸，化乳壮胃为上。盖吐乳呕乳，证有数般，有冷吐，有热吐，当审辨之。若吐自口角出。此是乳多不能消化，满则溢，此非病也，当服消乳丸。热吐则头额温，或有黄涎，五心热，小便赤少，或唇干而烦渴，多是暑月伤暑，或致此证，乳母服香薷散、五苓散，儿服香薷汤、五苓散。冷吐则清涎夹乳吐出，小便清而多，由乳母当风取凉解脱，致令风冷之气入乳，令乳变败，儿饮之则冷气入胃，故呕吐也。乳母宜捏去旧宿乳，服理中汤快气助胃之剂，次用酿乳法，茯苓半夏汤、加减观音散快胃之药。又有风痰吐者，乃是伤风不解，吐乳夹痰，久必生风，宜服青州白丸子、半夏散疏风化痰之剂。[25p]

Vomit

Vomit is accompanied by sound; to expel is to discharge milk and food. In general, infants should not be overfed. If they are full, they will overflow, leading to vomiting. Wet nurses, lacking knowledge, prioritize rapidly increasing the child's growth and neglect the appropriate feeding schedule. They may force feed the child while it is asleep, which becomes a source of illness, gradually worsening over time until vomiting occurs. In severe cases, it is advisable to gradually wean the child. The wet nurse should take medicinal herbs to regulate qi, and the child should take digestive pills to transform milk and strengthen the stomach. Vomiting from milk has several types: cold vomiting and hot vomiting, which should be carefully distinguished. If vomit comes from the corners of the mouth, it indicates that there is too much milk that cannot be digested, and if the stomach is full, it overflows; this is not an illness and can be treated with digestive pills. Hot vomiting is characterized by a warm forehead, possibly yellow saliva, a heated sensation in the palms and soles, scanty red urine, or dry lips with thirst. This is mostly due to summer heat or heat injury, leading to this symptom. The wet nurse should take herbal remedies like Xiangru San or Wuling San, while the child should take Xiangru Tang or Wuling San. Cold vomiting involves clear saliva mixed with milk being expelled, with frequent clear urination. This occurs because the wet nurse, exposed to wind, allows cool air to enter the milk, causing it to spoil. When the child ingests this, the cold air enters the stomach, resulting in vomiting. The wet nurse should remove old milk, take remedies to harmonize the stomach, and use methods to ferment the milk, combining it with Fuling and Banxia soup, or adjusting Guanyin powder to aid the stomach. Furthermore, if there is wind-phlegm vomiting, it results from unresolved wind and vomiting with phlegm; if this persists, it can lead to wind accumulation. This should be treated with Qingzhou Bai Wanzi or Banxia San to disperse wind and transform phlegm.[25p]

　　　　　泻泄

　　泻泄乃脾胃专病，凡饮食寒热三者不调，此为内因，必致泻泄。又经所论春伤风，夏飧泄；夏伤暑，秋伤湿，皆为外因，亦致泄泻。医者当于各类求之，毋徒用一止泻之方，而云概可施治，此则误儿，岂浅云耳？若不治本，则泻虽暂止而复泻，耽误既久，脾胃益虚，变生他证，良医莫救。
　　　　　霍乱吐泻

　　脾为中州，胃为水谷之海，乳哺入胃，脾能克化，然后水谷分其清浊，传变得宜，则无吐泻之患。凡小儿上吐不止，下泻不住，皆因内外伤侵，兼以调擭失常，乳食不节，遂使脾胃虚弱，清浊相干，蕴作而成。有先泻而后吐者，乃脾胃虚冷，其候先泻白水，吐亦不多，口气缓而神色慢，额前有汗，六脉沉濡，此为冷也。先吐而后泻者，乃脾胃有热，气促唇红，吐来面赤，脉洪而数，渴饮水浆，此为热也。冷热之分，须要详审。[26p]

Diarrhea

Diarrhea is a specific illness of the spleen and stomach. When the balance of three factors—cold, heat, and diet—is disturbed, this is an internal cause that will inevitably lead to diarrhea. Additionally, external causes such as summer heat causing summer diarrhea, and autumn humidity harming digestion can also lead to this condition. Physicians should address each type accordingly and not merely apply one method to stop the diarrhea, claiming it will treat all, as this misleads the child; is this not simplistic? If the root cause is not treated, the diarrhea may temporarily cease but will recur. If prolonged, the spleen and stomach will become increasingly deficient, leading to other conditions that good doctors cannot remedy.

Cholera with Vomiting and Diarrhea

The spleen is the center of the body, and the stomach is the sea of food and water. When milk enters the stomach, if the spleen can transform it properly, then the separation of the clear and turbid fluids will occur appropriately, thus preventing vomiting and diarrhea. In cases where children continuously vomit and have persistent diarrhea, this is caused by internal and external injuries, combined with the disruption of regular intake, leading to irregular feeding and resulting in weakness of the spleen and stomach, causing the clear and turbid to mix. If diarrhea occurs first followed by vomiting, this indicates cold in the spleen and stomach, characterized by white watery diarrhea, minimal vomiting, a gentle breath, and a slow countenance, with sweating on the forehead and a sinking, moist pulse—this suggests cold. If vomiting occurs first followed by diarrhea, this indicates heat in the spleen and stomach, with rapid breathing, red lips, a flushed face upon vomiting, a full and rapid pulse, and thirst for water—this suggests heat. The differentiation between cold and heat must be carefully examined.[26p]

　　伤风吐泻身温，乍寒乍热，气多粗，大便黄白色，呕吐乳食，完谷不消，时咳嗽，更五脏兼见证，宜先服钓藤散，后用益黄散、香朴散主之。及有吐泻，身热多睡，能食乳，饮水不止，吐痰，大便黄水，皆为胃虚热渴泻也，当生胃中津液以止其渴，后服发散止渴，多服白朮散、钓藤散。吐泻身凉，吐沫青白色，闷乱不渴，气肿露睛，当补脾，宜加减四君子汤、藿香散、银白散主之。夏月伤暑吐泻，手足厥冷者，理中汤、藿香正气散、五顺散、车前子散、不换金正气散可选而用之。如吐泻之证，有风搐欲成慢候，可看慢脾方论治之。古今图书集成医部全录卷四百三十五[27p]

In case of ailments like cold or diarrhea with a warm body, alternating between cold and heat, coarse breathing, yellowish-white stools, vomiting of milk or food, undigested grains, frequent coughing, and signs affecting the five organs, one should first take Diaoteng Powder, followed by Yihuang Powder and Xiangpu Powder to address the symptoms.

If there is vomiting and diarrhea, lethargy, the ability to consume milk, persistent thirst, expectoration, and yellow watery stools, these indicate a deficiency of stomach heat causing thirst and diarrhea. One should create fluids in the stomach to alleviate thirst, followed by dispersive treatments to quench thirst, such as taking Baizhu Powder and Diaoteng Powder.

In cases of cooling with vomiting and diarrhea, with frothy white saliva, discomfort without thirst, and bloating, the spleen needs to be nourished. One should consider modified Si Junzi Decoction, Huoxiang Powder, and Yinbai Powder for treatment.

During the summer, if one suffers from heat-related vomiting and diarrhea with cold hands and feet, options include Lizhong Decoction, Huoxiang Zhengqi Powder, Wushun Powder, Cheqianzi Powder, and Buhuanjin Zhengqi Powder. If symptoms of vomiting and diarrhea present with wind and severe contraction leading to chronic conditions, one may refer to the treatment strategies for weakened spleen syndrome.

This excerpt is part of the "Complete Compendium of Medical Books from Antiquity to Present," Volume 435.[27p]

小儿吐泻门

　　　　证治准绳 【明　王肯堂】

　　　　　吐泻

　　小儿吐泻并作，即名霍乱。有心痛而先吐者，有腹痛而先泻者，莫不由中焦而作。上焦主纳而不出；中焦主腐化水谷而生荣卫，灌溉百骸；下焦分别水谷，主出而不纳。脾居中州，胃为水谷之海，乳哺入胃，脾能克化，然后水谷分【脐上一寸有水分穴，】 传变得宜，岂有吐泻之患？凡小儿吐泻，皆因六气未完，六淫易侵，兼以调擭失宜，乳食不节，遂致脾胃虚弱，清浊相干，蕴作而然。有先泻而后吐者，乃脾胃虚冷，其候先泻白水，吐亦不多，口气缓而神色慢，额前有汗，六脉沉濡，此为冷也。有先吐而后泻者，乃脾胃有热，气促唇红，吐来面赤，脉洪而数，渴饮水浆，此为热也。冷热之分，要须详审。　　吐泻昏睡露睛者，胃虚热，白朮散、和中散主之。　　吐泻昏睡不露晴者，胃实热，钱氏玉露散、河间益元散主之。[28p]

Vomiting and Diarrhea in Children

Diagnosis and Treatment Guidelines
(Ming Dynasty - Wang Kengtang)

Vomiting and Diarrhea

When a child experiences both vomiting and diarrhea, it is referred to as "cholera." Those who have heart pain before vomiting or abdominal pain before diarrhea are all affected by issues in the middle energizer. The upper energizer is responsible for receiving and not expelling; the middle energizer is responsible for fermenting food and generating nourishment, irrigating the body; the lower energizer differentiates fluids, responsible for expelling and not receiving. The spleen resides in the center, and the stomach is the sea of food and drink. When milk enters the stomach, the spleen is able to transform it, allowing for appropriate distribution of fluids. How could there be issues of vomiting and diarrhea?

All cases of vomiting and diarrhea in children arise because the six qi have not matured, making them susceptible to the six excesses, combined with inappropriate dietary practices and irregular feeding, leading to spleen and stomach deficiency, where the clear and turbid mix, causing accumulation.

In cases where diarrhea occurs before vomiting, this indicates a cold deficiency of the spleen and stomach. The diarrhea is often characterized by white, watery stools, with little vomiting, a gentle breath, a slow demeanor, sweating on the forehead, and a deep, soft pulse—these are all signs of cold.

In cases where vomiting occurs before diarrhea, this suggests a heat condition in the spleen and stomach. Symptoms include rapid breathing, a red face after vomiting, a flooding and rapid pulse, and a thirst for water—these indicate heat.

The differentiation between cold and heat must be carefully examined.

For vomiting and diarrhea accompanied by lethargy with clear eyes, this indicates heat deficiency in the stomach; treat it with Bai Zhu San or He Zhong San.

For vomiting and diarrhea accompanied by lethargy without clear eyes, this indicates heat excess in the stomach; treat it with Qian's Yu Lu San or He Jian Yi Yuan San.[28p]

　　　　　夏秋治里

　　小儿初生三日内，吐泻壮热，不思乳食，大便乳食不消，或白色，是伤寒，当下之，并和胃。下用白饼子，和胃用益黄散主之。　　儿生三日已上至十日，吐泻身温凉，不思乳食，大便青白色，乳食不消，上实下虚也。更有五脏兼见证：肺，睡露睛喘气；心，惊悸饮水；脾，困倦饶睡；肝，呵欠烦闷；肾，不语畏明。当先视儿兼脏证，先泻其所实者而补其虚，如脾虚益黄散主之。此二证多病于秋夏也。[29p]

Treatment for Children in Summer and Autumn

When an infant is born and within three days, if they experience vomiting, diarrhea, intense heat, and lack of interest in milk or food, with stool that does not digest and is sometimes white, this indicates a case of cold damage. It should be treated immediately, and the stomach should be harmonized. Use white cake to aid digestion, and for harmonizing the stomach, use the benefit yellow powder as the main remedy.

If the child is three to ten days old, experiencing vomiting, diarrhea, with a body that feels warm or cool, and shows no interest in milk or food, with stool that is blue or white, indicating that the upper body is full while the lower body is deficient, one sees other symptoms related to the five organs: for the lungs, there is panting or difficulty in breathing; for the heart, there is anxiety and trouble when drinking water; for the spleen, there is fatigue and excessive sleep; for the liver, there is yawning and irritability; for the kidneys, there is a reluctance to speak and an aversion to light.

Priority should be given to observing the child and the symptoms related to the organs. First, treat the excess condition and then supplement the deficiency, such as using the benefit yellow powder for a deficient spleen. These two conditions are particularly common in summer and autumn.[29p]

　　凡小儿盛暑吐泻，邪热在下焦则泻，在上焦则吐，亡津必渴，用玉露散，虽吐，时时与啜之，过三日必愈。　　如身热脉大，小便黄，用五苓、益元各半，热汤调，温服之。如身凉脉细，小便青，早晨益黄散，午后玉露散。如过四五日困弱，宜异功散、和中散、开胃丸。如有风而泻，用防风、羌活，谓吐泻兼肝病风搐拘急也。　　有热而泻，用黄连、黄芩、大黄，谓吐泻兼心病身热也。　　有寒而泻，用附子，谓吐泻兼肾病身冷，或足胫寒而逆也。　　有湿而泻，用白朮、茯苓，谓吐泻兼本脏脾病，多睡体重昏倦也。　　有肺病而泻，用芍药、桂心，定喘，麦冬、人参，甚者多槟榔，大便不通加大黄。[30p]

For children suffering from heat-related vomiting and diarrhea in the summer, if the evil heat is in the lower jiao, it causes diarrhea; if it is in the upper jiao, it causes vomiting. The loss of fluids leads to thirst. Use Yu Lu San, and even if they vomit, give it to them in small sips over time, and they will surely recover in three days.

If the child has a high fever and a strong pulse, with yellow urine, use equal parts of Wu Ling and Yi Yuan, mixed with hot water and served warm. If the body is cool, with a weak pulse and blue urine, use Yi Huang San in the morning and Yu Lu San in the afternoon. If, after four or five days, they feel weak and fatigued, it is advisable to use Yi Gong San, He Zhong San, or Kai Wei Wan.

If there is diarrhea with wind, use Fang Feng and Qiang Huo, as this indicates vomiting and diarrhea alongside a wind-related liver condition causing convulsions and distress. If there is diarrhea accompanied by heat, use Huang Lian, Huang Qin, and Da Huang, indicating vomiting and diarrhea concurrent with heat-related heart illness.

If diarrhea is due to cold, use Fu Zi, indicating vomiting and diarrhea with kidney-related coldness, or cold in the feet and legs that is counteracting. If there is moisture-related diarrhea, use Bai Zhu and Fu Ling, indicating vomiting and diarrhea alongside spleen issues, characterized by excessive sleepiness and heavy fatigue.

If there is lung illness with diarrhea, use Shao Yao and Gui Xin to alleviate coughing, along with Mai Dong and Ren Shen; for severe cases, use more Bing Lang, and if there are issues with bowel movements, add Da Huang.[30p]

谓吐泻兼肺病喘嗽也。　　更详看病新旧，新则止之，久则有肠风之患。宜推陈致新，法当宣风散导过，后用入脏君臣药调之，宜益黄散。　　有小儿盛夏初秋，遇夜乘风，渴而饮水，过餐生冷果物，攻激肠胃，遂乃暴吐暴泻，传作手足俱痹，筋挛而痛，痛则神志不宁，以惊证治之，误矣。所谓筋遇寒则引缩；又以阳明养宗筋，属胃与大肠，因内伤生冷饮食，外感风邪，吐泻交作，胃气因虚，不能养其宗筋，亦致挛急。此证口气温，面色惨，脉沉锾，再以手按两膝腕下，见筋缩而引于皮间，是其候也。[31p]

It is said that diarrhea combined with lung disease causes coughing and wheezing. For diagnosis, one should look further into the conditions being new or old. If new, it should be treated to stop it; if prolonged, it may lead to the risk of intestinal wind. Therefore, it is advisable to push out the old and bring in the new, ensuring the treatment promotes dispersing the wind and guiding it outwards, followed by using tonics for the internal organs, specifically the monarch and minister herbs, and it is advisable to use Yi Huang San.

In young children during the beginning of summer to early autumn, if they are exposed to the wind at night, feel thirsty, drink water, and consume cold foods after meals, it can severely irritate their stomach and intestines, leading to sudden vomiting and diarrhea, which may then result in numbness of the hands and feet, with painful contractions of the muscles. If treated as a case of fright, it is mistaken. It is said that when muscles encounter cold, they contract and shorten; also, the Yangming channel supports the governing muscles, which are associated with the stomach and large intestine. Thus, internal injuries from consuming cold food and drink, combined with external wind, lead to simultaneous vomiting and diarrhea. The stomach qi becomes deficient and unable to nourish the governing muscles, causing contractions and urgency. In this case, the breath is warm, the face looks pale, the pulse is thick and submerged. Furthermore, when pressing on both knees and wrists, if one observes the muscles contracting and pulling towards the skin, these are the signs.[31p]

治以理中汤加附子，半生半炮，水姜熟煎，空心温服，更详虚实冷热为治可也。　　有数岁小儿忽患吐泻，始自夏秋昼近极热之地，解衣乘凉，夜卧当风之所致。盖先感热，后感冷，阴阳相抟，气射中焦，名为霍乱。《活人书》用香薷散调治，以其能分别水谷，升降阴阳。热多欲饮水者，五苓散。寒多不饮水者，理中丸。详此治法，得非欲平中焦乎？　　凡暑令吐泻，手足指热，作渴饮冷者，属阳证，宜清凉之剂。手足指冷，作渴饮热者，属阴证，宜温补之剂。凡病属阴证，误用寒凉者死，则手足青黯，或遍身皆然。[32p]

To treat with reformulated warm ginger water combined with prepared aconite, taken half raw and half processed, one should brew it with ginger until well-cooked and take it warm on an empty stomach, carefully noting the balance of deficiency and excess, as well as the interplay of hot and cold for treatment.

There are cases where young children suddenly suffer from vomiting and diarrhea, starting in the hot summer and autumn when they are exposed to extreme heat, removing their clothes to cool off, and then sleeping in a drafty area. They first contract heat, followed by cold, resulting in the interaction of yin and yang, causing qi to strike at the middle burner, which is called cholera. The "Book of Living" recommends the use of fragrant herb powder for treatment, as it can differentiate between food and water, regulating the ascending and descending of yin and yang. Those with excessive heat who desire to drink water should use the Five Licorice Powder. Those with excessive cold who do not want water should use the Reformulated Pill.

In dealing with this method of treatment, does it not aim to harmonize the middle burner? Generally, for summer-related vomiting and diarrhea, if the hands and feet are hot and there is thirst for cold drinks, it is a yang condition, thus requiring cooling agents. If the hands and feet are cold and there is thirst for hot drinks, it is a yin condition, thus requiring warming and tonifying agents. In all cases of yin conditions, if cold and cooling treatments are mistakenly applied, it can lead to death, evidenced by the hands and feet turning blue or dark, or this condition may spread throughout the body.[32p]

　　　　　冬春治表

　　伤寒吐泻身温，乍凉乍热，睡多气粗，大便黄白色，呕吐，乳食不消，时咳嗽，更有五脏兼见证，当煎入脏君臣药，先服大青膏，后服益黄散。如先曾下或无下证，慎不可下。此乃脾肺受寒，不能入脾也。　　洁古云：身温吐泻咳嗽，是风木入于脾，母虚其子亦弱，法当煎槟榔豆蔻汤下大青膏，后服益黄散。　　伤风吐泻，身热多睡，能食乳，饮水不止，吐痰，大便黄水，此为胃虚热渴吐泻也，当生胃中津液以止其渴；止后，用发散药。止渴，多服白朮散；发散，大青膏主之。　　洁古云：吐泻身热而渴，小便少者，五苓散主之。身热而呕者，当服白朮散，后煎槟榔木香汤下大青膏。[33p]

Winter-Spring Treatment Protocol

For conditions of cold damage presenting with symptoms such as fever, vomiting, diarrhea, intermittent chills and fever, excessive sleeping with strong breath, yellowish-white stools, vomiting, indigestion of milk and food, occasional coughing, and symptoms involving the five internal organs, one should boil the medicinal concoction for the internal organs and first take the Da Qing Gao (a specific medicinal preparation), followed by Yi Huang San (another medicinal powder). If there has been prior purging or no purging symptoms are present, one must be cautious and not purge. This indicates that the spleen and lungs are affected by cold, which prevents nourishment from entering the spleen.

The ancient text states: if there is a warm body with vomiting, diarrhea, and coughing, this suggests that wind wood has invaded the spleen, leaving the mother weak and the child likewise weak. The proper method is to prescribe a mixture of betel nut and cardamom to combat Da Qing Gao, followed by Yi Huang San.

For wind-cold with vomiting and diarrhea, alongside a warm body and excessive sleep, while still being able to eat milk, with continuous drinking and vomiting phlegm, and yellow watery diarrhea, this indicates a deficiency of the stomach with hot thirst along with vomiting and diarrhea. One should generate stomach fluids to alleviate thirst; after stopping the thirst, use dispersing medicines. To ease thirst, one can frequently take Bai Zhu San (a powder made from white atractylodes); to disperse, Da Qing Gao is the main remedy.

The ancient text also asserts: if there is vomiting and diarrhea accompanied by heat and thirst, with scant urination, it falls under the purview of Wu Ling San (a medicinal formula). If there is heat and vomiting, one should take Bai Zhu San first, and then boil the mixture of betel nut and wood incense to be combined with Da Qing Gao.[33p]

　　伤风吐泻，身凉吐沫，泻青白色，闷乱不渴，哽气，长出气，睡露睛，此伤风，荏苒轻怯，因成吐泻，当补脾后发散，大青膏主之。此二证多病于春冬也。　　洁古云：身凉吐泻不渴者，则知为寒，煎附子桂枝汤下大青膏。　　小儿伤于风冷，病吐泻，医谓脾虚以温补之，不已，复以凉药治之，又不能散。谓之本伤风，医者乱攻之，因脾寒积虚，内不能散，外不能解，至十余日，其证多睡露睛，身温，风在脾胃，故大便不聚而为泻，当去脾间风，风退则痢止，宣风散主之。后用史君子丸补其胃。亦有诸吐泻久不瘥者，则脾虚生风而成慢惊矣。　　吐泻过多，脾胃虚乏，欲生风候者，四君子加白附子减半，生姜煎服。[34p]

Wind injury causes vomiting and diarrhea, with coolness in the body, foamy spit, and stool that is greenish-white. There is a feeling of heaviness, no thirst, difficulty breathing, prolonged exhalation, and watery eyes upon waking. This is wind injury, characterized by weakness and fear, leading to vomiting and diarrhea. One should strengthen the spleen before dispersing. The main remedy is Da Qing Gao. These two patterns are often found in spring and winter.

Jie Gu said: When there is coolness in the body, vomiting and diarrhea occur without thirst, it indicates cold. Therefore, decoct a mixture of Fuzi and Guizhi to administer Da Qing Gao.

Children affected by wind and cold experience vomiting and diarrhea. The physician diagnoses it as spleen deficiency and prescribes warming tonics, but when it does not improve and cooling medications are used, it cannot disperse. This is considered a primary wind injury; the physician indiscriminately attacks it. Due to spleen cold and deficiency, the body cannot disperse internally nor resolve externally. After more than ten days, symptoms often include watery eyes and a warm body, with wind affecting the spleen and stomach, leading to loose stools. One should eliminate wind from the spleen; once the wind retreats, dysentery ceases. The main remedy for this is Xuan Feng San. Later, use Shi Jun Zi Wan to tonify the stomach. In cases of prolonged vomiting and diarrhea that do not heal, it indicates spleen deficiency leading to wind, resulting in chronic shock.

Excessive vomiting and diarrhea weaken the spleen and stomach and may lead to the emergence of wind. In such cases, prescribe Si Jun Zi Decoction with an increased dose of Bai Fuzi reduced by half, boiled with fresh ginger for consumption.[34p]

　　　　　身热泻黄多渴为热宜凉剂

　　曾氏云：先吐而后泻者，乃脾胃有热，气促唇红，吐来面赤，脉洪而数，渴饮水浆，此为热也。钱氏以吐泻身热，泻黄，多渴，作热病治，在夏秋用玉露散、益黄散相间服，在春冬用白朮散、大青膏相间服。
　　　　　肢冷泻青不渴为寒宜温药

　　曾氏云：先泻而后吐者，乃脾胃虚冷，其候先泻白水或白冻，吐亦不多，口气缓而神色慢，额前有汗，六脉沉濡，此为冷也。钱氏以吐泻身凉，泻青，不渴作寒病，在秋以益黄散主之，在冬春以益黄散、大青膏相间服。　　吐利四肢胀逆，脑门低陷，四君子加藿香、丁香、芍药等分煎服。
　　　　　肢温泻黄白似渴为寒热杂合病
　　钱氏治法，在夏秋用玉露散、益黄散相间服，在冬春用益黄散、大青膏相间服。[35p]

Body heat with yellow diarrhea and thirst is treated with cooling agents.

Zeng said: If one vomits first and then experiences diarrhea, it indicates heat in the spleen and stomach, with rapid breathing and red lips, vomiting leading to a flushed face, and a vigorous pulse. Thirst for water indicates heat. Qian suggested treating heat-related illnesses with a combination of Yulu powder and Yihuang powder in summer and autumn, and with Baizhu powder and Daqing paste in spring and winter.

Body cold with green diarrhea and no thirst is treated with warming medicine.

Zeng said: If one has diarrhea first and then vomits, it indicates cold due to deficiency in the spleen and stomach, presenting with clear or white diarrhea, minimal vomiting, gentle breath, slow complexion, sweating on the forehead, and a deep, soft pulse, indicating cold. Qian suggested treating cold-related illnesses with Yihuang powder in autumn and alternating Yihuang powder and Daqing paste in winter and spring. For symptoms of abdominal distension or reversal, with a sunken forehead, the Four Gentlemen decoction with additions of Huoxiang, Dingxiang, and Shaoyao should be prepared.

Body warmth with yellow or white diarrhea and thirst indicates a mixed condition of cold and heat.

Qian’s treatment method includes alternating Yulu powder and Yihuang powder in summer and autumn, and Yihuang powder and Daqing paste in winter and spring.[35p]

　　　　　宿食

　　钱氏云：吐泻乳不化，伤食也，宜下之。冯承务子五岁，吐泻壮热，不思食饮，钱氏见目中黑睛少而白睛多，面色晄白，曰：此子必多病。面色晄白者，神怯也。黑睛少者，肾虚也。黑睛属水，本怯而虚，故多病也。纵长成必肌肤不壮，不耐寒暑，易虚易实。脾胃亦怯，更不可纵恣酒欲，若不保养，不过壮年也。面上常无精神光泽者，如妇人之失血也。今吐利不食壮热者，伤食也。又虚怯不可下，下之虚，入肺则嗽，入心则惊，入脾则泻，入肾则益虚，但宜以消积丸磨化之，为微有食也。如伤甚则可下，不下则成癖也。若实食在内，亦可下也。下毕补脾必愈。随其虚实，无不效者。　　钱氏曰：吐乳泻黄是伤热乳，吐乳泻青是伤冷乳，皆当下之，此迎夺之法也。不若伤热者用五苓散以导其逆，伤冷者用理中汤以温其中，自然平复。　　脾经积滞未除，再为饮食所伤，不吐则泻，不泻则吐，宜以三棱散化积，守胃散和中。[36p]

宿食

Qian said: If there is vomiting and diarrhea with unprocessed milk, it indicates food damage, and it is appropriate to purge it. Feng Chengwu's child, five years old, experienced vomiting and diarrhea with high fever, showing no desire for food or drink. Qian observed that the child had more white in the eyes than black, and his complexion was pale, saying: This child must have many illnesses. A pale complexion indicates a lack of vitality. Few black eyes suggest renal deficiency. Since black eyes represent water, the inherent weakness and deficiency lead to frequent illness. If this continues into adulthood, the skin and flesh won't be robust, and he will be sensitive to cold and heat, easily fluctuating between deficiency and excess. The spleen and stomach are also weak, so indulgence in alcohol should be avoided. Without proper care, he won't survive past youth.

If the face lacks luster and spirit, it resembles a woman who has lost blood. Now, if there is vomiting and diarrhea with high fever and no appetite, it signifies food damage. Additionally, if there is weakness, purging should be avoided; if purged while weak, it leads to coughing if it enters the lungs, fright if it enters the heart, diarrhea if it enters the spleen, and further deficiency if it enters the kidneys. It is better to dissolve a digestive pill to provide some nourishment. If the damage is severe, purging may be necessary; otherwise, it can lead to a lasting condition. If there is impacted food inside, purging is also possible. After purging, reinforcing the spleen will ensure recovery. There is no case where this does not work, according to the state of deficiency and excess.

Qian further stated: Vomiting milk and diarrhea with a yellow tint indicates damage from hot milk; with a blue tint, it indicates damage from cold milk. Both should be purged as a method of addressing the issue. However, for damage from heat, use Wuling Powder to guide the reverse effect; for cold damage, use Lizhong Decoction to warm the interior, which will naturally restore balance.

If there is still stagnation in the spleen channel and then further food damage occurs, if there is no vomiting it leads to diarrhea; if no diarrhea, it leads to vomiting. It is advisable to use Sanddough Powder to dissolve stagnation and to guard the stomach with Hezhong Powder to harmonize the interior.[36p]

　　　　　心腹痛

　　儿冷热不调，乳哺不节，使阴阳清浊之气，相干而变乱肠胃间，则成霍乱而心腹痛者，冷气与真气相击，或上攻心，下攻腹，故痛。
　　　　　禁忌

　　郑氏云：小儿吐泻，因外伤风冷，内伤乳食，或儿啼未定，气息未调，以乳饲之，气逆于上则停滞胸膈，致令呕吐；气逆于下则伤脾胃，致令泄泻；上下气逆，吐泻俱作。凡小儿只吐不泻者逆，其吐必有痰，发惊者十无一生。若只泻不吐，或吐泻俱发者，日久不退，亦变阴癎。治之乃暂断其乳，轻者周时，重者三日，宜频与稀粥，服药速效，十全八九。[37p]

Abdominal Pain

When a child suffers from irregular temperature and breastfeeding, the interplay of clear and turbid energies disrupts the stomach and intestines, leading to cholera and abdominal pain. Cold energy clashes with vital energy, sometimes attacking the heart from above and sometimes the abdomen from below, resulting in pain.

Contraindications

Zheng states: When a child has vomiting and diarrhea due to external cold or wind injuries, or internal injury from milk and food, or if the child’s crying is unsettled and their breath is unregulated, if they continue to breastfeed, the breath may reverse upwards, causing stagnation in the chest and leading to vomiting; if it reverses downwards, it harms the spleen and stomach, resulting in diarrhea; when breath reverses both up and down, vomiting and diarrhea occur simultaneously.

In cases where a child only vomits without diarrhea, this is a sign of reversal; there will be phlegm with the vomiting, and those who show signs of shock, ten out of one hundred do not survive. If a child only has diarrhea without vomiting, or experiences both together, and this persists over time, it may transform into convulsions. Treatment involves temporarily stopping breastfeeding; for mild cases, a few hours, and for severe cases, three days. It is advisable to frequently provide diluted porridge and administer medication for quick effect, with a success rate of eighty to ninety percent.[37p]

或者不信是言，以小儿借乳为命，不肯暂断，然乳固不可断也，殊不知因乳所伤得之者，若再以伤乳乳之，如抱薪救火，药何功之有？其间有不断服药得安者，盖轻患也。亦有因轻致重，夭横者多矣。　　《活幼心书》云：小儿吐泻不止，大要节乳，徐徐用药调治必安。节者，撙节之义，一日但三次或五次，每以乳时不可过饱，其吐自减，及间以稀粥投之，亦能和胃。屡见不明此理，惟欲进药以求速效，动辄断乳三四日，致馁甚而胃虚，啼声不已，反激他证。盖人以食为命，孩非乳不活，岂容全断其乳？然乳即血也，血属阴，其性冷，吐多胃弱，故节之。医者切须知此，乳母亦宜服和气血调脾胃等药。愚意不若儿大能食者全断之，待其平复；儿小不能饮食者，但节之可也。[38p]

It may be doubted whether this is true, but the life of a child depends on milk, and they are unwilling to stop it even temporarily. However, milk indeed cannot be stopped, yet they do not realize that those harmed by milk, if they continue to consume it recklessly, are like trying to put out a fire with more kindling—such remedies will be of no benefit at all. Among those who continue taking medicine and find peace, their ailments are likely minor. Yet there are many who, due to light issues, become gravely ill.

The "Book of Nurturing Young Hearts" states that when a child experiences continuous vomiting and diarrhea, it is imperative to reduce milk intake, administering medicine slowly for stabilization. Reducing means to cut back; for a day, offering only three or five times, and not overfeeding at each time. This will alleviate vomiting, and occasionally giving thin porridge can also help harmonize the stomach. It is often observed that those who do not grasp this principle rush to give medicine in hopes of quick results, abruptly stopping milk for three to four days, leading to extreme hunger and weakened stomachs, resulting in unending cries, which aggravates the condition.

Food is essential to life, and a child cannot survive without milk; how can one completely stop their milk? Yet milk is akin to blood, which is yin in nature and cold. Excessive vomiting leads to a weak stomach, thus the need to reduce it. Physicians must understand this thoroughly, and wet nurses should also take medicine that harmonizes qi and nourishes the blood to regulate the spleen and stomach. My humble opinion is that for older children who can eat, one should completely stop milk until they recover; for younger ones who cannot drink or eat, it is sufficient to only reduce the milk.[38p]

　　　　　吐

　　吐沫及痰或白绿水，皆胃虚冷。吐稠涎及血，皆肺热。吐水不止者，属心痛胃冷。吐水心痛者，虫痛。口中吐沫水者，后必虫痛。　　面晄白无精光，口中气冷，不思食，吐水，当补脾，益黄散主之。　　冬月吐蛔，多是胃虚寒而虫作吐，用钱氏白朮散加丁香二粒，方可用理中汤去甘草加乌梅、肉川椒。　　呕吐皆主脾胃。古人谓脾虚则呕，胃虚则吐是也。呕者有干无物，吐者有物无干。[39p]

Vomiting

Saliva and phlegm or white-green water indicate a deficiency and coldness of the stomach. Thick saliva and blood indicate heat in the lungs. Continuous vomiting of water corresponds to heart pain and stomach coldness. If vomiting water accompanies heart pain, it indicates pain from parasites. If one is spitting out watery saliva from the mouth, they will likely experience parasitic pain later.

A pale face with a lack of vitality, cool breath in the mouth, no desire for food, and vomiting water suggest a need to tonify the spleen; the formula "Yi Huang San" should be used. During winter, if there is vomiting of roundworms, it is mostly due to cold deficiency of the stomach and the worms causing vomiting. Use the "Qian's Bai Zhu San" with two pieces of clove, and for this, one can apply the "Li Zhong Tang" without licorice, adding black plum and Sichuan pepper.

Vomiting is primarily related to the spleen and stomach. The ancients said that if the spleen is deficient, there is vomiting, and if the stomach is deficient, there is vomiting as well. In cases of nausea, there may be dry without substance, while vomiting involves substance without dryness.[39p]

若手足指热，喜饮热汤，或睡而露睛，皆胃气虚弱也，用异功散。若手足指热，饮冷，或睡不露睛，属胃经实热也，用泻黄散。若作渴少食，或小便色赤，胃经虚热也，用七味白朮散。大凡婴儿在乳，母尤当节饮食，若乳母停食，亦能致儿吐泻，故不可不慎也。　　论吐之原，难以枚举，有冷吐、热吐、积吐、伤风嗽吐、伤乳吐，其吐则同，其证有异，各述于后：　　冷吐：乳片不消，多吐而少出，脉息沉微，面白眼慢，气缓神昏，额上汗出。此因风寒入胃，或食生冷，或伤宿乳，胃虚不纳而出。[40p]

If the fingers and toes are warm, preferring to drink hot soup, or sleeping with eyes exposed, this indicates a weakness of stomach qi, and one should use Yigong Powder. If the fingers and toes are warm, drinking cold, or sleeping without exposing the eyes, this pertains to excess heat in the stomach channel, and one should use Xiehuang Powder. If experiencing thirst with decreased appetite, or if urination is reddish, this signifies weakness and heat in the stomach channel, and one should use Qiwèi Baizhu Powder. Generally, for infants on milk, the mother should particularly regulate her diet. If the wet nurse stops eating, it can also cause the child to vomit or have diarrhea, so care is essential.

Regarding the causes of vomiting, they are difficult to enumerate: there is cold vomiting, hot vomiting, accumulated vomiting, vomiting due to wind cold, and vomiting due to improper milk. Although the act of vomiting is the same, the symptoms differ, which will be discussed later.

Cold vomiting: Milk curds do not digest, frequent vomiting with little outgoing, pulse is deep and weak, face pale with slow eyes, breathing is gentle with mental dullness, and sweat appears on the forehead. This occurs due to wind-cold entering the stomach, or consuming raw and cold food, or harming previously ingested milk, leading to stomach weakness and inability to retain food, resulting in vomiting.[40p]

宜温胃去风，除宿冷，用当归散，水、煨姜、陈皮煎服；或间投冲和散、理中汤，及姜橘汤、定吐饮。如诸药不效，以参香饮治之。　　热吐：面赤唇红，吐次少而出多，乳片消而色黄，遍体热甚。或因暑气在胃，或食热物，精神不慢而多烦躁，此热吐也。宜解热毒，用大顺饮；温熟水空心调下；并五苓散、小柴胡汤，并加姜汁缓服，及香薷散主之。误服热药，先投菉豆饮解之，次服止吐之剂。　　积吐：眼泡浮，面微黄，足冷肚热，昼轻夜重，儿大者脉沉缓。[41p]

Should warm the stomach to dispel wind and remove lingering cold, using Danggui powder, decocted with water, ginger, and aged tangerine peel; or intermittently administer Chōnghé powder, Lǐzhōng decoction, and ginger-tangerine soup, or Dingtǔ drink. If these remedies are ineffective, treat with Ginseng and Xiang beverage.

Hot vomiting: face red and lips purple, vomiting occurs less frequently but in large amounts, milk has dissipated and the color is yellow, the body is very hot all over. This may be due to heat in the stomach from summer heat or consuming hot foods, with a restless spirit and much agitation; this is considered hot vomiting. One should dispel heat toxins with Dàshùn drink; use warm water to adjust to an empty stomach; also employ Wǔlíng powder and Xiǎo Cháihú decoction, adding ginger juice for gradual consumption, and use Xiāngrǔ powder for it. If hot medicines have been mistakenly consumed, first administer Lú Dòu drink to counteract, then take remedies to stop vomiting.

Accumulated vomiting: eyelids swollen, slightly yellow face, cold feet with a hot abdomen, lighter during the day and heavier at night, with a deep and slow pulse in older children.[41p]

此宿冷滞脾，故吐黄酸水；或有清痰，脉实而滑，为食积所伤，吐酸馊气；或宿食并出，儿小者，哯乳不化是也。先用五苓散，姜汁温汤调下和解；次以乌犀丸主之；最小者投三棱散、化癖丸。　　伤风嗽吐：有热生风，有风生痰，痰结胸中，肺气不顺，连嗽不止，和痰吐出。此为嗽吐痰壅而作，乃为实证。宜去风化痰，先投清肺饮，次小柴胡汤为治。若嗽久而肺虚，土不生金，故面白唇燥，干嗽干呕而无痰，可温补为上，用茯苓厚朴汤、惺惺散、如意膏为治。　　伤乳吐：才乳哺后即吐，或少停而吐。此因乳饮无度，脾气弱不能运化，故有此证。譬如小器盛物，满则溢。治法宜节乳，投三棱散。[42p]

This lodging is cold and stagnates the spleen, hence the vomiting of yellow sour water; there may also be clear phlegm, with a firm and slippery pulse, caused by food accumulation, leading to the vomiting of sour and rotten gas; or undigested food may also expel, especially in small children, who vomit milk that does not digest. First, use Five Ling Powder, mixed with ginger juice and warm water to harmonize; then administer Black Rhinoceros Pill to manage it; for the very young, administer Three-Edge Powder and Transforming Abnormal Pill.

As for wind-cold cough with vomiting: there may be heat generating wind, or wind creating phlegm, which blocks the chest, causing unimpeded lung qi and persistent coughing. This is due to phlegm obstruction causing cough and vomiting, indicating a solid condition. It would be advisable to eliminate wind and transform phlegm; first administer Clear Lung Drink, followed by Minor Chaihu Decoction for treatment. If coughing persists and the lungs become deficient, leading to a lack of generation from the earth, the face may appear pale and lips dry, with a dry cough and dry retching without phlegm. In this case, warming and tonifying is optimal, using Poria and Magnolia Decoction, Awakening and Clarity Powder, and Ruyi Paste for treatment.

For breastfeeding-related vomiting: if vomiting occurs immediately after nursing or shortly thereafter, this arises from excessive milk intake and a weak spleen unable to process it, hence this condition. It is like a small container filled to the brim, leading to overflow. The treatment should involve moderating milk consumption and administering Three-Edge Powder.[42p]

　　此外又有风痰吐，乃是伤风不解，吐乳夹痰，若多必要生风，宜服青州白丸子、半夏散。疏风下痰之剂，皆可服之。　　毒气吐，详见后。
　　夹惊吐，张涣三香丹之类。
　　疳积吐，出《本事方》。
　　凡霍乱吐不止者，伏龙肝细末二钱，以芦稷米炒黄煎汤调下，立止。或用白扁豆炒过煎汤调下亦好。若白扁豆嫩苗更好。
　　　　　寒吐

　　小儿寒吐者，由乳母当风取凉解脱，致令风冷入乳变败，儿若饮之，故呕吐也。乳母当食后捏去旧宿败乳，急服理中汤，次用酿乳法。其候是寒清痰夹乳吐出是也。凡有此候，服药不效，胃气将绝，药不能下，当服灵砂丸；如大便通，宜来复丹。二药常用，验。　　寒吐之证，面目胀，额汗出，脉沉迟微，寒气停于胃，故胃不纳而吐出也。哕逆者，由胃气虚甚，过服克伐，使清气不升，浊气不降，以致气不宣通而作也。风寒在胃者，用理中丸。胃气虚者，六君子汤。[43p]

Additionally, if there is phlegm and wind causing vomiting, it results from unresolved exterior wind, which leads to the expulsion of milk mixed with phlegm. If this occurs frequently, wind is likely to be generated; it is advisable to take Qingzhou Baiwanzi or Banxia San. Any remedy that disperses wind and relieves phlegm can be administered.

For toxic gas causing vomiting, refer to later sections.

For vomiting due to fright, remedies similar to Zhang Huan's Sanxiandan can be used.

For vomiting due to accumulation of food (disease), refer to the "Ben Shi Fang".

For persistent vomiting in cases of cholera, take two qian of finely powdered Fulong liver mixed with roasted Coix seed and simmered in broth, then consume. Alternatively, using roasted white hyacinth beans mixed in broth is also effective, especially young white hyacinth bean sprouts.

Cold Vomiting

For cold vomiting in infants, it results from the wet nurse experiencing wind and becoming chilled, causing wind and cold to enter the breast milk and spoil it; thus, when the child drinks it, vomiting occurs. The wet nurse should eliminate spoiled leftover milk after meals and urgently take a regulating concoction, followed by the method of brewing milk. The symptoms involve cold clean phlegm mixed with milk being vomited. If there are these symptoms and the medicine is ineffective, the stomach qi may be almost exhausted; in such cases, Ling Sha Wan should be taken. If bowel movements are regular, then Lai Fu Dan may be appropriate. The two medicines are commonly used.

In cases of cold vomiting, the facial complexion appears swollen, sweat may be present on the forehead, and the pulse is deep, slow, and weak; cold energy stagnates in the stomach, preventing acceptance and thus leading to vomiting. Hiccups arise from excessive deficiency of stomach qi, due to overuse of purging methods, which prevent clear qi from rising and turbid qi from descending, leading to unsteady qi flow. If wind-cold is present in the stomach, use Li Zhong Wan. If there is stomach qi deficiency, use Liu Jun Zi Tang.[43p]

风凉所致者，宜捏去败乳，急服理中丸，次服酿乳法。若呕吐清涎夹乳而吐，小便清利，用大安丸。若因乳母食厚味，用东垣清胃散。若乳母饮醇酒，用葛花解酲汤，饮烧酒服冷米酢三五杯。乳母食生冷而致者，用五味异功散。乳母停食者，母服大安丸，子服异功散。乳母劳役者，子母俱服补中益气汤。乳母怒动肝火者，用加味逍遥散。乳母郁怒伤脾者，用归脾汤。乳母脾虚血弱者，用六君、芎、归，其子亦服三五滴。气血虚而乳热者，子母俱服八珍散，仍参热吐霍乱治之。[44p]

For conditions caused by cool wind, it is advisable to pinch off spoiled milk, urgently take the Li Zhong Wan, and then use the fermented milk method. If there is vomiting of clear phlegm mixed with milk, and clear, frequent urination, use the Da An Wan. If the wet nurse has eaten rich foods, use the Dong Yuan Qing Wei San. If the wet nurse drinks strong alcohol, use the Ge Hua Jie Cheng Tang; drink three to five cups of cold rice vinegar with strong liquor. If the wet nurse has eaten raw and cold foods, use the Wu Wei Yi Gong San. If the wet nurse stops eating, the mother should take the Da An Wan, and the child should take the Yi Gong San. If the wet nurse is overworked, both mother and child should take the Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang. If the wet nurse's anger stirs up liver fire, use the Jia Wei Xiao Yao San. If the wet nurse is upset and injures the spleen, use the Gui Pi Tang. If the wet nurse has a weak spleen and blood deficiency, use Liu Jun, Xiong, and Gui, and the child should also take three to five drops. For conditions of qi and blood deficiency with hot milk, both mother and child should take the Ba Zhen San, and still address the heat, vomiting, and dysentery.[44p]

　　　　　热吐

　　小儿秋夏伏暑，多有热吐，其吐黄涎，头额温，五心热，小便或赤而少，乃热吐也。或干呕无物，宜香薷饮。　　小儿热吐者，因多食甘甜炙煿之物，或乳母膏粱厚味，胃经积热，或夏间暑气，内伏于胃所致。若肌肉瞤动，烦热作渴者，暑伤胃气也，先用香薷散，次用竹茹汤。若吐乳色黄，不能受纳者，胃经有热也，先用泻黄散，次用人参安胃散。若吐出酸秽者，乳食内停也，用保和丸。吐乳不消者，胃气弱也，用异功散。吐而少食，腹痛欲按者，脾气虚也，用六君子加木香。凡诸证当验其手指，热则胃热，冷则胃寒。热用泻黄散，寒用理中汤；不热不寒，异功散调之。[45p]

Heat Vomiting
